PREFACE. 



This tenth volume of Somerset Marriage Registers in- 
cludes the remaining portion of the Registers of the important 
parish of St. Mary's, Taunton, down to the year 1812. Of this 
Mr. Bates undertook the transcription. For Bishop's Hull, 
and, in part, for Halse, Mr. Seager has been responsible. 

It is intended that Volume XI shall be devoted to various 
country Parish Registers. The Marriage Registers of St. 
James, Taunton, have already been transcribed, and will be 
printed in a later volume. 4 O^QO/f C 

The usual contractions have been made use of — 

w.=widower or widow. p.=of the parish ot. 

s.=spinster, single woman, co.=in the county of. 

or son of. dioc.=in the diocese of. 

b.=bachelor, or single man. /?V.=marriage licence. 
d.=daughter of. 

The reader must remember that the printed volumes 
are not "evidence" in the legal sense. Certificates must be 
obtained from the local clergy in charge of the Registers. 

It is the Editors' wish to print two volumes annually, 
and thus to make a steady and substantial progress in the 
work of preserving our ancient Parish Registers from the 
risks of destruction or loss to which they are constantly 
exposed, even in the best circumstances, so long as their con- 
tents remain in manuscript only. They will welcome help in 
the work of transcription. 

W. P. W. P. 

H.W.S. 

E. H. B. 
December, 1907-

SOM — X. 



Marriages at Bishop's Hull, 

1562 to 1812. 

Note. — Volume I is a narrow folio, written on vellum, in fairly good 
condition, except the first three pages, which are torn and much 
rubbed ; it is covered with brown paper, and its contents are : — 
Marriages, Baptisms, and Burials. On the first page is written : 
—"This is the Register Book of the parish of Hilbishopp's, newly 
written in parchment according to the Statute made in A". 
1598." 

Volume II is a narrow folio on vellum, in vellum cover, in fairly good 
condition, but the first page much thumbed and somewhat damp- 
stained. The following Somerset entry may here be noticed : — 
"John N[arton], of [Hilbishop ?], in the said county, was sworne, 
Parrish Register of the said pish, by me, Richard Bouett [Esq. ?], 
one of the Peace within the said county, according to an Act of 
Par[liament on] that behalfe provided. Wittness my hand this 
4th day of April], 1656, Ri. Bouett, John Grudge, William Lane, 
Richard Kingland." [The signatures are evidently autographs.] 

"This is the Regester Booke for the parish of Hilbishopp, newly 
made according to an Act of Parlement procurd for that porpos. 
In the yeare ot our lord God, 1653, for the marages An publica- 
tions of the parish of H[ilbishop]. John Norton, Regestar, 1656." 

Volume III is a long folio written on vellum, in good condition, but 
pages at end much stained. Contents :— Marriages, Baptisms, 
and Births. On cover in modern writing: — "The Register Book 
for the Parrish of Bishop's Hull, Anno Domini 1695-1734. 
Marriages and Baptisms :— The Register, commencing on the 
inside of the cover, is headed : — "This is the Register Booke for 
the Parrish of Hillbishopps, made according to A Statute in that 
Cause made and povided. Januaiy the 1st, Anno Domini 1695." 

Volume IV is a very long folio written on paper and bound in calf — 
in good condition. Marriages are entered at one end and 
Baptisms at the other. 

Volume V is a paper folio of printed forms containing Marriages 
and Banns, bound in somewhat ragged sheep, and dated 1754. In 
good condition, but ink much faded. 

Volume VI is a paper folio of printed forms containing Marriages 
and Banns — bound in sheep. In very good condition. 

These extracts have been made by leave of the Rev. R. C. W. 
Raban.

[^Pencil note here, Marriages from 1734 to 1754 missing.'] 
[There are several blank pages before the beginning of the 
Births and Baptisms where the last entries are September 1734, 
February 1733, and May 1736. This Register has evidently 
been carelessly written, as there are so many gaps in it. The 
Register of Marriages from 1734 to 1754 is not missing but 
entered in a book of Baptisms, and continued [after ending with 
IT ^4) from 1790/0 1798.]

Marriages at Halse, 

1559 to 1812. 

Note.— Volume I consists of several sheets of vellum, of a large quarto 
size, loose and without cover, neatly written in double columns. 
The contents are Christenings, Burials, and Marriages, from 1559 
to 1652. This book is not entered in the Parish Register Abstract 
ofi83i. 
Volume II is a narrow folio of loose vellum leaves, with a loose 
parchment wrapper, containing Baptisms, Burials, and Marriages, 
1653 to 1685. 
Volume III is a similar book of loose vellum leaves, containing 
Baptisms, Burials, and Marriages, 1696 to 1753, ^'so in a loose 
parchment wrapper. The earlier entries are in a very confused 
state. 
Volume IV is the usual printed folio, bound in sheep-skin, con- 
taining forms for Banns and Marriages, 1754 to 1812, irregularly 
entered, but in fairly good condition. 
The copy has been made from a transcript provided by the Rev. 
F. J. Montgomery, and is now printed with his permission. 
Volume I. 
" The table of those p'sons which have been married within 

the p'rish of Halse from the beginninge of our Sovraigne Lady 

Queene Elizabeth's Raigne that now is, Dei gra., Anglie 

Fraunc. et Hib'ne, Regina fidei Defensor, &c."
